try {
    var setCMPCookie = function(name, value, domainName, days){
        if(!!domainName){
            var domain = ";domain="+domainName;
        }
        if(!!days){
            //Below variable is one day time in mili seconds.
            var _oneDayinMS = 24*60*60*1000;
            var d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (days*_oneDayinMS));
            var expires = ";expires="+d.toUTCString();
        }
        document.cookie = name+"=" +value + ( ( expires ) ? expires : '' ) + ( ( domain ) ? domain : '' ) + ";path=/";
    };

    var optOutCookieName = "optout";
    var optOutCookieAge = 365;
    var dsmiCookieName = "dsmi";
    var dsmiCookieAge = 365;
    var dateOneTrust = new Date();
    var urlParamsCmp = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

    dateOneTrust.setTime(dateOneTrust.getTime() + (optOutCookieAge * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));

    // Set default cookies (opted out by default)
    setCMPCookie(optOutCookieName, '1', window.location.host, optOutCookieAge);

    // GDPR callback to set cookies based on EU user status
    if (window.TimesGDPR && window.TimesGDPR.common && window.TimesGDPR.common.consentModule && window.TimesGDPR.common.consentModule.gdprCallback) {
        window.TimesGDPR.common.consentModule.gdprCallback(function(dataObj) {
            if (dataObj.isEUuser === false) {
                // Non-EU user: set cookies to 0
                setCMPCookie(optOutCookieName, '0', window.location.host, optOutCookieAge);
            } else if (dataObj.isEUuser === true) {
                // EU user: set cookies to 1
                setCMPCookie(optOutCookieName, '1', window.location.host, optOutCookieAge);
            }
        });
    }

    function setOnAcceptOptOut(isCCPA = false) {
        if(isCCPA) {
            setCMPCookie(dsmiCookieName, '0', window.location.host, dsmiCookieAge);
        }
        setCMPCookie('ckns_policyV2', '1', window.location.host, 365);
        if (window.localStorage) {
            window.localStorage.setItem('ccpaGdprPopupShown', '1');
        }
    }
    
    function setOnRejectOptOut(isCCPA = false) {
        if(isCCPA) {
            setCMPCookie(dsmiCookieName, '1', window.location.host, dsmiCookieAge);
        }
        setCMPCookie('ckns_policyV2', null , window.location.host, 365);
        if (window.localStorage) {
            window.localStorage.setItem('ccpaGdprPopupShown', '1');
        }

            attachGoogleCMPListners();
        }

    function attachGoogleCMPListners() {
        window.googlefc.callbackQueue.push({
            'CONSENT_DATA_READY':
            () => __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2.2, (consentData, success) => {                    
                // 1. Check if GDPR applies
                if (consentData.gdprApplies === true) {
                    // 2. Check if the consent process was completed successfully
                    if (consentData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete' || consentData.eventStatus === 'tcloaded') {
                        // 3. Check if the user has consented to personalized ads (Purpose 1)
                        if (consentData.purpose && consentData.purpose.consents && consentData.purpose.consents["3"] === true) {
                            // User has consented to personalized ads, unset the opt out cookie
                            setOnAcceptOptOut();
                        } else {
                            // User did not consent to personalized ads, set the opt out cookie
                            setOnRejectOptOut();
                        }
                    } else {
                        // Consent process was not completed
                        setOnRejectOptOut();
                    }

                } else {
                    // GDPR doesn't apply, proceed with standard behavior or do not require consent
                    setOnAcceptOptOut();
                }
            })
        });

        // Queue the callback on the callbackQueue.
        window.googlefc.callbackQueue.push({
            'INITIAL_CCPA_DATA_READY':
            () => {
            switch (googlefc.ccpa.getInitialCcpaStatus()) {
                case googlefc.ccpa.InitialCcpaStatusEnum.CCPA_DOES_NOT_APPLY:
                setOnAcceptOptOut(true);
                break;
                case googlefc.ccpa.InitialCcpaStatusEnum.NOT_OPTED_OUT:
                setOnAcceptOptOut(true);
                break;
                case googlefc.ccpa.InitialCcpaStatusEnum.OPTED_OUT:
                setOnRejectOptOut(true);
                break;
            }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Call the function to ensure the script is loaded
    loadGPTScript();
} catch (err) {
  console.log("cmp_js error", err);

TimesApps.popupManger2 = function popupManagerHigherOrderPopups() {
    window.TimesApps = window.TimesApps || {};

    TimesApps.PopupV2 = function(name, showPopCallback , priority, data) {
      const dataObj = data || {};
      this.id = name;
      this.lastShownTimeStamp = dataObj.lastShownTimeStamp
        ? dataObj.lastShownTimeStamp
        : null;
      this.showPopCallback = showPopCallback;
      this.priority = priority;
      // this.status;
      this.userActionStatus = null;

      // this.forceRepeat = dataObj.forceRepeat;
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.showPopCallback = function() {
      return this.showPopCallback();
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.getDetailsPopUp = function() {
      return { ...this };
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.onReadyCallback = function(status) {
      this.ready = status;
      if (status === 3) {
        this.setStatus(false);
      }
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.isReady = function() {
      return this.ready;

    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.onShowCallback = function(status) {
      this.shown = status;
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.getStatus = function() {
      return this.status;
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.setStatus = function(status) {

    };

    TimesApps.PopUpV2Manager = (function() {
      /*
          1. Register overlay
          2. Decide overlay priority
          3. show overlay
  
  
          Register overlay
              - registerOverlay
                  - return onReadyCallback
                  - all popup's call onReadyCallback to mark status, they are ready to be called
              - read priority from config
              - create priority queue
  
          Decide overlay priority
              - read priority queue
              - call if 1st is ready
                      - if status OK  - call
                      - else if not needed to be called, call Next
              -
  
          Show overlay
              - save state in Localstorage
                  - show - true/false
                  - timestamp
  
  
          Config
              - popup list
              - priority for each
              - show frequency
      */
  
      const config = {
        browserStorageKey: 'popUpManagerHigherOrderPopUps',
      };
  
      const constants = {
        HRS_IN_DAY: 24,
        MINS_IN_HR: 60,
        SEC_IN_MIN: 60,
        MilliSEC_IN_SEC: 1000,
      };
  
      const fn = {
        _docReady(forcefully = false) {
          (function() {
            const referrer = document.referrer;
            try {
              if(forcefully) {
                const data1 = JSON.parse(
                  localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
                );
                if (data1.actualData &&
                  Array.isArray(data1.actualData) &&
                  data1.actualData.length > 0 &&
                  (TimesApps.PopUpList[data1.actualData[0].name] &&
                  TimesApps.PopUpList[data1.actualData[0].name].getDetailsPopUp()?.id === 'interstitial')){
                    let pageViewsAfterGDPR = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                    if (!pageViewsAfterGDPR && isNaN(pageViewsAfterGDPR)) {
                        pageViewsAfterGDPR = 0;
                    }
                    localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', pageViewsAfterGDPR + data1.burninterval);
                    return;
                  }
              }
              if (window.localStorage && window.toi_client_side_settings) {
                  if(window.localStorage && localStorage.getItem("ccpaGdprPopupShown") === '1'){
                      let pageViewsAfterGDPR = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                          if (!pageViewsAfterGDPR && isNaN(pageViewsAfterGDPR)) {
                              pageViewsAfterGDPR = 0;
                          }
                          localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', pageViewsAfterGDPR + 1);
                      }
                let pageViews =
                  localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR') &&
                  parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                let data = JSON.parse(
                  localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
                );
                fn._saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews);
                if (
                  data &&
                  Date.now() - data.time >
                  data.burntime * constants.SEC_IN_MIN * constants.MilliSEC_IN_SEC
                ) {
                  localStorage.removeItem(config.browserStorageKey);
                  localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', 1);
                  pageViews = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                  data = null;
                }
                if (!data) {
                  window.toi_client_side_settings.time = Date.now();
                  data = window.toi_client_side_settings;
                  data.actualData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data.priority));
                  data.actualData.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
                  if (!(localStorage.getItem("autoCcpaGdprPopupShown"))){
                    data.nextPageView = 1 + data.burninterval;
                  } else {
                    data.nextPageView = 1;
                  }
                  fn._saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews);
                }
                config.burninterval = data.burninterval;
                config.burntime = data.burntime;
                config.data = data;
                if (config.data.actualData &&
                  Array.isArray(config.data.actualData) &&
                  config.data.actualData.length > 0) {
                  if(config.data.nextPageView - (config.burninterval + 1) === pageViews || forcefully){
                    if (!forcefully){
                      document.addEventListener('popup_manager_ready', function(event) {
                        if (!(TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name] && config.data.actualData[0].status === 1)) {
                          return fn._docReady(true);
                        }
                        TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name].showPopCallback()
                      });
                    } else {
                      if (!(TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name] && config.data.actualData[0].status === 1)) {
                        return fn._docReady(true);
                      }
                      TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name].showPopCallback()
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            } catch(ex){
              console.log(ex, "Popup manager Error")
            }
          })();
        },
        _init() {
          console.log('Pop up manager is initialtized');

                  if(typeof cbfn === 'function'){

        _saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews) {
          if(data?.actualData &&
            Array.isArray(data?.actualData) &&
            data.actualData.length > 0 && pageViews && pageViews > 0){
            // eslint-disable-next-line guard-for-in, no-restricted-syntax
            data.actualData.some((singleData, index) => {
                if (singleData.status === 1) {
                    const shouldRepeat = singleData.forceRepeat || singleData.repeat;
                    if (shouldRepeat) {
                        singleData.priority = data.actualData[data.actualData.length - 1].priority + 1;
                        singleData.status = 0;
                        data.actualData.push(singleData);
                    }
                    data.actualData.shift();
                }
                if(data.actualData && Array.isArray(data.actualData) && data.actualData.length > 0){
                  singleData = data.actualData[0];
                  if (data.nextPageView === pageViews) {
                      singleData.status = 1;
                      data.nextPageView = pageViews + data.burninterval + 1;
                      return true;
                  }
                }
            });
            localStorage.setItem(config.browserStorageKey, JSON.stringify(data));
          }
        },
        _registerPopUp(id, callBack) {
          let callbacks = {};
          try{
            const popUp = fn._createPopUpObject(id, callBack);
            if (!popUp) return null;
            callbacks = {
              onReadyCallback: fn._onReadyCallback.bind(popUp),
              onShowCallback: fn._onShowCallback.bind(popUp),
              onUserActionCallback: popUp.onUserActionCallback,
              getDetail: fn._getDetails.bind(popUp),
            };
            popUp.callbacks = callbacks;
            TimesApps.PopUpList[id] = popUp;
            let data = JSON.parse(
              localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
            );
            let actualData = Array.isArray(data.actualData) && data.actualData.length > 0 ? data.actualData.map((d)=> d.name).sort() : [];
            let popupList = Object.keys(TimesApps.PopUpList).sort();
            if (actualData.join() === popupList.join()){
              document.dispatchEvent(TimesApps.popupManagerFullyInitilizedEvent);
            }
          } catch (err) {}
          return callbacks;
        },
        _getDetails(){
            return this.getDetailsPopUp();
        },
        _onReadyCallback(status) {
          this.onReadyCallback(status);
        },
        _onShowCallback(status) {
            /*
             * popup displayed
             */
            debugLogs('*** onShowCallback', this, status);
            this.onShowCallback(status);
            fn._setStatusInStorage(this, status);
          },
          _setStatusInStorage(obj, status) {
            const data = fn._getStatusFromStorage();
            const index = fn._getIndex(data.actualData, obj.id);
            data.actualData[index].lastShownTimeStamp = Date.now();
            data.actualData[index].shown = status;
            data.actualData[index].atPageView = parseInt(
                localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'),
                10,
            )
            if( data?.actualData && Array.isArray(data?.actualData) && data?.actualData.length){
              data.actualData.shift();
              fn._setStatusFromStorage(data);
            }
            if (status === false) {
              fn._docReady(true);
            }
          },
          _getIndex(data, named) {
            let index = -1;
            if(data){
                Object.keys(data).forEach((key, i) => {
                    if (data[key].name === named) {
                        index = i;
                    }
                });
            }
            return index;
          },
        _createPopUpObject(id, showCallback = null) {
            const popUpdata = {};
            const data = fn._getStatusFromStorage();
            if (!(data && data.actualData)){
                return null;
            }
            const { priority, lastShownTimeStamp, name } = data.actualData.find(
              item => item.name === id,
            ) || {};
            if (name){
              popUpdata.lastShownTimeStamp = lastShownTimeStamp;
              return new TimesApps.PopupV2(name, showCallback, priority, popUpdata);
            }
        },
        _isPopuManagerRunningInSession() {
          if (localStorage.getItem("pageViewsAfterGDPR") && fn._getStatusFromStorage()) return true;
          return false;
        },
        _setStatusFromStorage(data) {
            localStorage.setItem(config.browserStorageKey, JSON.stringify(data));
        },
        _getStatusFromStorage() {
          const jsonData = localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey);
          let data;
  
          try {
            data = JSON.parse(jsonData) || {};
          } catch (e) {
            data = null;
            //console.log('popupManager, JSON error');
          }

          return data;
        },
      };

      fn._docReady();
      const regiteredPopup = window.TimesApps.PopUpV2Manager.cmd || [];
      setTimeout(()=>{
        fn._init();
      },100)

      const api = {
        cmd: {
            push: function(callback){
                if(typeof callback === 'function'){
                    callback();
                }
            }
        },
        regiteredPopup: regiteredPopup,
        register(id, showCallback) {
          return fn._registerPopUp(id, showCallback);
        },
        isPopuMangerRunning() {
          return fn._isPopuManagerRunningInSession();
        },
        reloadPopupManager(forcefully) {
          return fn._docReady(forcefully);
        },
      };

      return api;
    })();

            if(callback && typeof callback === 'function'){

                window.requestIdleCallback(callback);
              } else {
                setTimeout(callback,0)
              }
            }
        };

        function loadJs(src) {
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.type = "text/javascript";
          script.src = src;
          script.async = true;
          script.defer = true;
          if(src && src.includes('_es6_module')) {
              script.type = "module";
            } else if(!(src && (src.includes('geoapi')))) {
              script.noModule = true;
            }
          document.body.appendChild(script);
        }  
        _chunks.forEach(function(src) {
          setTimeout(function(){
              loadJs(src)
            },0)
          });

        if(typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.TimesApps) {
            var functionsToCall = ["ResetFirstFoldScroll", "initCLSHandling"];
            var functionsToCallWhenIdle = [
              "loadGrowthRXsdk",
              "popupManger2", 
              "showInterstitial",
              "loadScriptsOnceAdsReady",
              "loadTpSdk",
              "toiPlusEvents"
            ];
            if(false) {
              functionsToCallWhenIdle = [
                "loadScriptsOnceAdsReady",
              ];
            }
            var callTimesAppsFn = function (fnName, useIdleCallback) {
              if (typeof window.TimesApps[fnName] === "function") {
                if (useIdleCallback) {
                  callOnBrowserIdle(window.TimesApps[fnName]); 
                } else {
                  window.TimesApps[fnName]();
                }
              }
            };
            functionsToCall.forEach(function (fn) {
                callTimesAppsFn(fn, false);
            });
            functionsToCallWhenIdle.forEach(function (fn) {
                callTimesAppsFn(fn, true);
            });
        }
    }

    window._loadDelayedResources = function(){
      // console.log('Document Ready State', document.readyState);
      if (!_delayedResourcesLoaded && typeof window !== 'undefined') {
        _delayedResourcesLoaded = true;
        debugLogs('########## Calling _loadDelayedResources in React App: ', (performance.now()/1000).toFixed(2)+'seconds');
        if(false) {
          loadStateJSON("", loadResources);
        } else {
          loadResources();
        }
        
      }
    }

    if(_callDelayedResourcesImmediately){
      // TODO: Trigger the event for delayed load in ga4
      window._loadDelayedResources();
    }
    else {
      // Commented due to ads impacted due to it.
      // document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
      //   setTimeout(window._loadDelayedResources, 0);
      // });
      setTimeout(() => {
        debugLogs('########## Calling _loadDelayedResources via settimeout - fail fallback: ', (performance.now()/1000).toFixed(2)+'seconds');
        window._loadDelayedResources();
        // TODO: Trigger the event for delayed load in ga4
      }, 6000);
    }
